REFERENCE  (J,PR/C,80,044604,2009)                                1425700100034 
           (C,2007NICE,1,335,2007) Preliminary data in graphical  1425700100035

FACILITY   (SYNCH,2ZZZCER)                                        1425700100037 
SAMPLE     Enriched 233U samples, six samples were used           1425700100038 
           (92-U-233,ENR=0.9901)                                  1425700100039 
           (92-U-234,ENR=0.0074)                                  1425700100040 
           (92-U-235,ENR=0.0023)                                  1425700100041 
           (92-U-238,ENR=0.0004)                                  1425700100042 
           Chemical form - oxide U3O8                             1425700100043 
           Mass ranging from 7.86 to 16.6 g                       1425700100044 
           Areal density ranging from 4.04E+7 to 8.46E+7 at/barn  1425700100045 
DETECTOR   (FISCH) Measurement was performed with a fission       1425700100046 
           ionization chamber, specifically built for fission     1425700100047 
           cross section measurements on radioactive U isotopes   1425700100048 
           and other actinides at n-TOF.                          1425700100049 
METHOD     (TOF) Very low repetition rate of 0.4 Hz, long         1425700100050 
           flight path of 185 m and very high neutron flux        1425700100051 
           10E+5 n/cm2/pulse at 200 m allow for very precise      1425700100052 
           measurement over a large energy range.                 1425700100053 
MONITOR    (92-U-235(N,F),,SIG)                                   1425700100054 
MONIT-REF  (,M.Chadwick+,3,ENDF/B-VII.0,,2006)                    1425700100055 
           GeV/c protons from the CERN proton synchrotron         1425700100056 
           incident on a natural Pb target.                       1425700100057 
ANALYSIS   Cross section determined for each energy bin           1425700100058 
           relative to monitor reaction                           1425700100059 
CORRECTION Correction for different counting efficiencies of      1425700100060 
           233U and 235 U samples, originating from different     1425700100061 
           sample thicknesses was made by simulation  using       1425700100062 
           Monte Carlo package FLUKA. Calculated correction       1425700100063 
           factor was 3.3%.                                       1425700100064 
           Correction for dead time, significant above            1425700100065 
           300 keV, overall correction less than 2%               1425700100066
